### [1] [On the dilaton gravity of analogue black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11046)
*Paolo Castorina,Alfredo Iorio,Jakub Kris,Mohaddese Shams Nejati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了哪些标量-引力模型能够再现超导量子电路等平台中实现的二维类比黑洞，并分析了这些模型中霍金温度的状态依赖性特征，指出当前实验中的类比黑洞并不对应已知的标量-引力模型，从而限制其理论价值；同时提出可反向从已知模型出发，推导实验实现所需条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索能再现实验平台（如超导量子电路）中二维类比黑洞的标量-引力模型，并理解其霍金温度状态依赖性的物理起源与理论意义。

Method: 基于理论建模与数值分析，识别标量-引力模型需满足的合理假设，分析霍金温度T与熵S的动力学/运动学解耦特性，并对比已知模型与实验对应关系。

Result: 发现所研究的类比黑洞不匹配任何已知标量-引力模型；揭示了二维类比黑洞可具有状态依赖或无关的霍金温度，而四维黑洞无此特性；提出反向设计思路：从成熟标量模型出发推导实验约束条件。

Conclusion: 当前实验实现的二维类比黑洞在理论上缺乏对应的标准标量-引力描述，其理论启发有限；未来重点应转向依据可靠理论模型来指导和约束实验实现。

Abstract: We investigate which dilaton gravity models can reproduce the typical two dimensional analogue black holes realized in platforms such as superconducting quantum circuits. We identify the most reasonable assumptions these models must satisfy, and determine the dilaton models for which the state-dependence of the Hawking temperature, T, can be switched on and off, a feature that is absent in four dimensional black holes. When the analogue black hole exhibits state-independent temperature, as in the cases considered here, the kinematics governing T decouples from the dynamics underlying S. Our numerical analysis reveals that the given analogue black holes do not correspond to known dilaton gravity models, limiting their usefulness for extracting theoretical insights. We then show that the logic can be easily reversed: starting from established well known dilaton models, one can derive the conditions that laboratory implementations must satisfy. This shifts the challenge from the theoretical perspective to the experimental realization.

</details>


### [2] [CMB Birefringence from Vacuum Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11065)
*Nemanja Kaloper*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需超轻轴子即可解释宇宙微波背景偏振旋转的新机制，即光子穿越拓扑不同的暗区真空界面时获得的几何界面相位（Pancharatnam相），该效应由壁支撑的电磁Chern-Simons相互作用归一化决定，并受低能有效理论中涌现的1-形式对称性保护。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释观测到的CMB偏振旋转（Δϑ ∼ 10⁻³ rad）通常依赖于超轻轴子的晚期动力学，但作者质疑这一必要性，旨在寻找更基本、不依赖轻场的物理解释。

Method: 基于拓扑真空结构和低能有效场论，引入界面处的电磁Chern–Simons项，利用1-形式对称性分析其保护机制，并区分绝热轴子壁与非绝热极限下的离散Pancharatnam相。

Result: 发现偏振旋转可作为真空界面的几何效应自然出现，适用于任意薄壁情形（轴子重或不存在），且旋转角与红移和光子频率无关（低于紫外截断），从而将宇宙双折射重新诠释为暗区真空结构的探针。

Conclusion: 宇宙双折射并非必然源于轻标量场动力学，而可源于暗区真空的拓扑界面几何，为检验暗 sector 真空结构提供了新观测量和理论框架。

Abstract: Hints of cosmic microwave background polarization rotation ($Δ\vartheta \sim 10^{-3}$ rad) are commonly attributed to late-time dynamics of ultralight axions. We show that such ultralight degrees of freedom are not required. Polarization rotation naturally arises as a geometric interface phase acquired when photons cross interfaces between topologically distinct dark sector vacua. The effect is a discrete phase shift fixed by the normalization of a wall-supported electromagnetic Chern--Simons interaction and protected by an emergent $1$-form symmetry of the low energy effective theory. This mechanism reproduces the familiar adiabatic rotation induced by light axion domain walls, but persists for arbitrarily thin walls where the axion is heavy or absent. In this regime the rotation manifests as a Pancharatnam phase localized at vacuum interfaces, independent of redshift and photon frequency below a natural ultraviolet cutoff. Cosmic birefringence thus emerges as a probe of vacuum structure in the dark sector, rather than of light-field dynamics.

</details>


### [3] [Confinement in Holographic Theories at Finite Theta](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24732)
*Rashmish K. Mishra*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过全息引力描述研究了具有非零真空角的强耦合禁闭规范理论的去禁闭-禁闭相变，构建了一个简化的五维模型，其中体标量场模拟真空角效应，并确定了紫外和红外边界的适当边界条件；结果表明临界温度随真空角二次减小，拓扑磁化率在临界温度处急剧下降，且相变速率受高能变形相关性影响；若真空角随时间变化，可显著改变早期宇宙中的相变历史并诱导超冷却，进而影响引力波信号的可观测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解强耦合规范理论中真空角对相变行为的影响，尤其是与格点QCD结果的一致性，以及其在早期宇宙动力学和引力波现象学中的应用。

Method: 采用全息引力对偶方法，构建一个五维简化模型，用体标量场模拟真空角，设定合适的UV/IR边界条件（IR条件受高维Wilson圈收缩周期启发），在小红外反作用极限下分析相变行为。

Result: 临界温度随真空角二次减小、拓扑磁化率在Tc处锐减、相变速率依赖于高能变形的相关性（相关变形增强速率，无关变形减弱甚至导致禁闭相失稳）；时变真空角可引发超冷却并调控相变时机，从而改变引力波信号的峰值频率和功率。

Conclusion: 该全息模型成功再现了格点QCD的关键特征，并揭示了真空角在宇宙学相变及引力波探测中的关键调控作用，为探索QCD相变与早期宇宙物理提供了新视角。

Abstract: A strongly coupled confining gauge theory with a non-zero vacuum angle undergoing a deconfinement to confinement phase transition is studied in the holographic gravitational description. A simplified five-dimensional setup is constructed where a bulk scalar models the effect of the vacuum angle, and the suitable boundary conditions on the ultra-violet (UV) and the infra-red (IR) boundaries are identified. The IR boundary condition is motivated by higher dimensional examples where the bulk scalar comes from a Wilson loop on a shrinking cycle. In this five-dimensional dual geometry, and in the limit of small backreaction in the infra-red, the critical temperature for the phase transition is shown to reduce quadratically with the vacuum angle, matching lattice results. The topological susceptibility has a sharp reduction across the critical temperature, also matching lattice results. The rate for the phase transition is estimated as a function of the vacuum angle, and is seen to be enhanced (reduced) when the field theory has a relevant (irrelevant) deformation at high energies. Crucially, for the irrelevant case, the confined phase can get destabilized for a range of parameters. In the context of early universe dynamics, if the vacuum angle is time-dependent, the transition history changes strongly: the deconfined phase can last till much lower temperatures than naively expected, and one can trigger a transition to the confined phase by a change in the vacuum angle, thus providing a controlled way to generate supercooling. As a phenomenological application, the peak frequency and the power of resulting gravitational wave signal from bubble collisions change, affecting their visibility in detectors. Possible generalizations of the scenario are discussed.

</details>


### [4] [Towards the Realization of the Dark Dimension Scenario in Hořava-Witten Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11068)
*Ralph Blumenhagen,Antonia Paraskevopoulou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨了Hořava-Witten理论作为暗维度场景的具体实现，指出通过对E8壁上对称性反常抵消的分析，可缓解质子衰变过快等问题，并联系M理论的Emergence Proposal，推测可通过单圈Schwinger积分获得标量势、规范耦合与普朗克尺度的模依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决暗维度场景中质子衰变速率过快等关键问题，并统一解释暗能量尺度与标准模型规范耦合大小。

Method: 基于Hořava-Witten理论框架，结合Calabi-Yau流形上带阿贝尔因子的向量丛，分析E8壁上的对称性反常抵消；引入M理论Emergence Proposal的无限远距离极限，并外推BPS饱和振幅结果，用单圈Schwinger积分估算模依赖性。

Result: 发现对称性反常抵消可改善质子衰变问题；导出一个特殊无限远距离极限，对应于M理论Emergence Proposal的Hořava-Witten类比；推测标量势、规范耦合和普朗克尺度的模依赖性可能由塔状态的单圈Schwinger积分给出。

Conclusion: Hořava-Witten理论在暗维度场景中具有重要潜力，其与反常抵消、Emergence Proposal及谱几何的结合，为统一理解粒子物理与宇宙学参数提供了新路径。

Abstract: It has been suggested that Hořava-Witten theory could provide a concrete realization of the Dark Dimension Scenario. In this context, the observable Standard Model sector is naturally localized in the micron-sized large dimension, which is the interval in the eleventh direction. Considering Calabi-Yau manifolds supporting generic vector bundles including also abelian factors, we point out that symmetric tadpole cancellation on the $E_8$ walls has the potential to ameliorate some of the issues of such a realization, including too fast proton decay. By taking not only the hierarchically small value of the dark energy but also the size of the Standard Model gauge couplings into account, one is driven to a special infinite distance limit, which is the Hořava-Witten analogue of a limit recently at the focus of the M-theoretic Emergence Proposal. Extrapolating results obtained for BPS-saturated amplitudes, we speculate about the possibility of obtaining the moduli dependence of the scalar potential, the gauge couplings and the Planck scale by simple one-loop Schwinger integrals over towers of states.

</details>


### [5] [A Monte Carlo Study of the Dipolar Universality Class in Three Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11573)
*Akira Matsumoto,Yu Nakayama,Toshiki Onagi,Slava Rychkov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引入一个忠实实现序参量横向约束的晶格模型和一种结合局部Metropolis更新与全局零模更新的马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛算法，对三维强偶极相互作用铁磁体的偶极普适类相变进行了蒙特卡洛模拟研究，观测到连续相变，并估算了临界指数、Binder比等普适量，验证了临界点处旋转不变性的涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 偶极普适类虽被理论（重整化群）和实验研究多年，但蒙特卡洛模拟研究极少，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 构建满足序参量横向约束的晶格模型；设计结合局部Metropolis更新（保约束）与全局零模更新的MCMC算法；在最大达48×48×48的立方晶格上开展模拟。

Result: 观测到无序相到有序相的连续相变；获得关键临界指数、Binder比等普适量的数值估计；发现临界点处出现旋转不变性。

Conclusion: 成功实现了对偶极普适类的高精度蒙特卡洛模拟，为该普适类提供了独立于重整化群和实验的数值基准，并证实了临界旋转对称性的恢复。

Abstract: The dipolar universality class describes the phase transition in 3D ferromagnets with strong dipolar interactions, as first discussed by Aharony and Fisher in the 1970s. While this universality class has been studied theoretically using renormalization group methods, as well as experimentally, little is known about it from Monte Carlo simulations. In this paper we aim to bridge this gap. We introduce a lattice model that faithfully implements the transverse constraint on the order parameter. We introduce a Markov Chain Monte Carlo algorithm which involves a combination of local Metropolis updates preserving the constraint, and a global update of the zero mode. We perform simulations on cubic lattices up to volume $48\times 48 \times 48$. We observe a continuous phase transition between the disordered and ordered phases. We obtain estimates of universal quantities such as the main critical exponents and the Binder ratio, and compare them with results from other techniques. We also investigate the emergence of rotation invariance at the critical point.

</details>


### [6] [Positivity in Massive Spin-3/2 EFTs and the Planck-Suppressed Neighbourhood of Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11072)
*Jay Desai,Diptimoy Ghosh,Saurabh Pant*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了质量为m的Majorana自旋3/2粒子的有效场论在m→0极限下的行为，发现只有当引力子存在且四费米子接触相互作用被调至N=1超引力所要求的值时，该极限才平滑；当忽略引力子t道极点时，推导出非正向树图色散界，并确定了满足幺正性和解析性的有效耦合参数空间：当m远小于普朗克质量时，允许区域是围绕超引力点的一个有界、普朗克压制邻域，其体积随m^6/M_Pl^6缩小；当m接近M_Pl时，该区域无界；引入轻标量/赝标量自由度（如Polonyi模型）并不扩大允许的接触耦合空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解质量自旋3/2粒子有效理论如何平滑趋近于严格零质量极限，该极限要求超引力框架；检验低能有效描述与紫外完备性（如超引力）之间的兼容性。

Method: 基于幺正性与解析性，采用非正向、树图级色散关系方法，推导质量自旋3/2粒子四费米子接触算符的约束；忽略引力子t道极点以聚焦接触项行为；分析不同质量尺度（尤其是m ≪ M_Pl和m ∼ M_Pl）下耦合参数空间的几何特征；拓展至含轻标量/赝标量场的情形。

Result: 当m ≪ M_Pl时，允许的有效耦合构成一个以超引力点为边界的、体积∝ m⁶/M_Pl⁶ 的有界区域；超引力点位于该区域边界上；当m→0时区域收缩至一点，复现无质量极限结论；当m→M_Pl时区域无界；加入Polonyi型标量/赝标量场后，其耦合也受类似约束，但不扩大原有接触耦合的允许空间。

Conclusion: 质量自旋3/2粒子的有效理论仅在精细调节至超引力值附近且质量足够小时才具一致性；其紫外完成必须包含引力，且低能行为强烈受限于解析性与幺正性；这为超对称破缺能标与引力尺度的关系提供了新的理论约束。

Abstract: It is well known that a strictly massless spin-$3/2$ particle can interact consistently only within supergravity. Recently, positivity arguments have shown that an effective field theory of a massive Majorana spin-$3/2$ particle admits a smooth $m \to 0$ limit only if a graviton is present and the four-fermion contact interactions are tuned to the values dictated by $\mathcal{N}=1$ supergravity. In this work, we investigate how this limit is approached at finite mass. Assuming that the graviton $t$-channel pole can be discarded, we derive non-forward, tree-level dispersive bounds on massive spin-3/2 contact operators and determine the region of effective couplings consistent with unitarity and analyticity. For sufficiently small $m$, we find that the allowed parameter space forms a bounded, Planck-suppressed neighbourhood of the supergravity point, defined by the supergravity values of the four-fermion couplings. The supergravity point lies on the boundary of this region. In the regime $m \ll M_{\rm Pl}$, the volume of the allowed region scales parametrically as \[ \mathrm{Vol} \sim \frac{m^{6}}{M_{\rm Pl}^{6}} \, , \] and shrinks to zero as $m \to 0$, smoothly reproducing the massless-limit results. The allowed region becomes unbounded when mass approaches the Planck scale. We further analyze the effect of including additional light scalar and pseudo-scalar degrees of freedom, motivated by the Polonyi model, and find that their couplings are also bounded in a way similar to the contact couplings and that it doesn't enlarge the allowed contact coupling space.

</details>


### [7] [Compact space catalysis of false vacuum decay and Schwinger effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11081)
*Saquib Hassan,John March-Russell*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了D维紧致空间中零温假真空衰变，发现当体积低于临界值时，存在一种不同于Coleman O(D)泡的新bounce解，该解通常导致衰变速率呈指数增强；该bounce在洛伦兹符号解析延拓后，在小体积下产生均匀场构型，稍大体积下产生准均匀构型，并非嵌入假真空背景中的薄壁或厚壁泡；作者通过涨落本征谱验证了其符合假真空衰变特征，并讨论了体积增大时从均匀到准均匀的过渡及其实时间解释，最后将其应用于标量场模型和紧致空间中(1+1)d轴子电动力学的类Schwinger效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究紧致空间中零温假真空衰变的新机制，特别是传统Coleman泡解在小体积下可能失效的情形。

Method: 分析D维紧致空间中假真空衰变的bounce解，研究其解析延拓至洛伦兹符号后的物理图像，计算涨落本征谱以验证其衰变特性，并将该解应用于标量场模型与(1+1)d轴子电动力学。

Result: 发现体积低于临界值时存在新型bounce解，导致指数增强的衰变速率；该解对应均匀或准均匀场构型，而非传统气泡结构；其涨落谱满足假真空衰变要求；并成功应用于两个具体物理模型。

Conclusion: 紧致空间中小体积下的假真空衰变由新型bounce主导，揭示了传统无限空间结论的局限性，拓展了对量子隧穿与真空不稳定性在受限几何中行为的理解。

Abstract: We study zero-temperature false vacuum decay in $D$ compact spatial dimensions and show that for volumes below a critical value a new bounce solution, different from Coleman's celebrated $O(D)$ bubble, mediates the decay process, and typically leads to an exponentially enhanced decay rate. The bounce, when analytically continued to Lorentzian signature, nucleates a homogeneous field configuration for spatial volumes below a critical value, and quasi-homogeneous configurations for slightly larger volumes, and is not of the form of a thin or thick-walled bubble embedded in a false vacuum background. We explicitly show that the new bounce has the necessary features associated with false vacuum decay, following from its eigenvalue spectrum of fluctuations. The cross-over from homogeneous to quasi-homogeneous solutions as the spatial volume is increased is discussed, as is a real-time interpretation of the bounce. We apply this bounce to the study of a scalar field model, as well as a close cousin of the Schwinger effect that applies to $(1+1)d$ axion electrodynamics in compact space.

</details>


### [8] [Analytic Bootstrap of the Veneziano Amplitude](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11084)
*Shi-Lin Wan,Shuang-Yong Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了Veneziano振幅是基于色散求和规则、幺正性和少量弦论输入的对偶自举方法的唯一结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Veneziano振幅在对偶自举框架下的唯一性，结合色散关系与弦论特性。

Method: 利用色散求和规则作为矩序列，并将弦论输入（如单值性条件或分裂与隐零条件）精确融入振幅假设中。

Result: 在所有阶上解析地证明了Veneziano振幅是满足条件的唯一解。

Conclusion: 色散求和规则与特定弦论约束的结合，使对偶自举具有足够刚性以唯一确定Veneziano振幅。

Abstract: We analytically prove, to all orders, that the Veneziano amplitude is the unique outcome of a dual bootstrap based on dispersive sum rules, unitarity, and a small amount of additional stringy input. This stringy input can be either the string monodromy condition or the recently uncovered splitting and hidden-zero conditions. A key ingredient in our proofs is to interpret the dispersive sum rules as sequences of moments. Equally important is the precise incorporation of the extra stringy input into the amplitude ansatz, which makes the analytic bootstrap sufficiently rigid to fix the amplitude uniquely.

</details>


### [9] [Stochastic inflation from a non-equilibrium renormalization group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11096)
*Sebastián Céspedes,Thomas Colas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从两个互补的角度研究了随机暴胀理论中的系统性修正计算问题：一是基于粗粒化描述的约化密度矩阵推导长波模式的有效场论，二是研究密度矩阵随粗粒化尺度变化的重整化群流；两者均导出了包含耗散与扩散项的广义福克-普朗克方程，并能系统纳入次领头阶修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机暴胀理论中，如何从第一性原理出发系统地计算可控修正仍是一个重要未解问题。

Method: 1) 从粗粒化描述的约化密度矩阵出发，构建长波模式的开放有效场论，利用薄壳近似保证时间局域性，超哈勃尺度下动态恢复空间局域性；2) 建立直接作用于密度矩阵的Polchinski型重整化群方程，研究其随粗粒化尺度的演化。

Result: 得到含耗散与扩散项的开放有效场论，其中扩散在红外极限占优；导出广义福克-普朗克方程，可系统包含次领头阶随机动力学修正；两种方法结果一致，并与Schwinger-Keldysh描述相容。

Conclusion: 本文为随机暴胀提供了首个从第一性原理出发、兼具系统性与可控性的有效理论框架，统一了开放量子系统与重整化群视角，为高精度宇宙学预测奠定基础。

Abstract: Understanding stochastic inflation, and in particular the systematic computation of controlled corrections from first principles, remains an important open problem. In this work, we address this problem from two complementary perspectives. First, we derive the effective field theory governing long-wavelength modes from the reduced density matrix of a coarse-grained description. In this framework, locality in time follows from the thin-shell approximation, while locality in space is recovered dynamically in the super-Hubble regime. The resulting open effective field theory contains both dissipative and diffusive operators, with diffusion dominating as the coarse-graining scale is pushed into the infrared. This construction reproduces the usual Fokker-Planck equation at leading order and allows us to compute its corrections, including subleading contributions to the stochastic dynamics. Second, we study the evolution of the density matrix under changes of the coarse-graining scale. We show that this flow is governed by a Polchinski-type renormalisation group equation formulated directly for the density matrix. Dissipative and diffusive operators are generated dynamically along the flow, and the resulting effective action matches the Schwinger-Keldysh description. We derive a generalised Fokker-Planck equation directly from the renormalisation group flow, systematically incorporating subleading corrections and recovering the results obtained in the open effective field theory approach.

</details>


### [10] [Aharonov--Casher effect from a supersymmetric N=1 D=4 model with Kalb--Ramond Lorentz-violating background: a SUSY-preserving mechanism via the Fayet--Iliopoulos term](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11493)
*L. A. S. Nunes,C. A. S. Almeida*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个N=1、D=4超对称规范模型，通过洛伦兹破缺的Kalb-Ramond背景动力学诱导出Aharonov-Casher（AC）效应所需的偶极相互作用，且不破坏超对称性；该模型利用手征超场与阿贝尔规范超场间的Chern-Simons型耦合及Fayet-Iliopoulos项，并通过偶极项在非相对论极限下复现AC哈密顿量，从而实现了超对称性与AC效应在四维中的相容。

Conclusion: Aharonov-Casher效应与未破缺的四维超对称性并非本质互斥，其兼容性取决于具体模型构造；本文提供了首个显式实现——即在超对称性严格保持的前提下，AC相互作用可作为低能有效现象自然出现。

Abstract: The Aharonov--Casher (AC) effect describes the geometric phase acquired by a neutral particle carrying a magnetic dipole moment moving in an external electric field. In supersymmetric gauge theories it is often argued that exact supersymmetry enforces the vanishing of anomalous magnetic dipole moments, suggesting that the AC interaction may be incompatible with unbroken supersymmetry in four dimensions. In this work we show that this conclusion is model-dependent. We construct an $N=1$, $D=4$ supersymmetric gauge model in which a Lorentz-violating Kalb--Ramond background induces dynamically the dipole interaction responsible for the AC effect while leaving the supersymmetry algebra intact. The model couples a chiral superfield to an Abelian gauge superfield through a Chern--Simons--type interaction supplemented by a Fayet--Iliopoulos term. A duality identification between the symmetric combination $S+S^\dagger$ of the chiral superfield and the Kalb--Ramond superfield strength allows the antisymmetric tensor background to enter the supersymmetric dynamics without breaking supersymmetry. Integrating out the auxiliary $D$ field generates dynamically an effective dipole interaction of the form $\barψσ^{μν}F_{μν}ψ$. In the nonrelativistic limit the resulting equation of motion reproduces the Aharonov--Casher Hamiltonian for a neutral fermion. The effective magnetic dipole moment is expressed in terms of the parameters of the model and can be mapped onto tensor coefficients of the fermion sector of the Standard Model Extension. Our results therefore provide an explicit realization of a four-dimensional supersymmetric theory in which the Aharonov--Casher interaction emerges dynamically while supersymmetry remains exact in the presence of Lorentz violation.

Abstract: In this paper, we determine the relativistic bound-state solutions for the Dirac oscillator (DO) in the curved spacetime of a cloud of strings in $(3+1)$-dimensions, where such solutions are given by the four-component normalized Dirac spinor and by the relativistic energy spectrum. However, unlike in literature, here, we work with the spacetime in two different forms/configurations, that is, both in its original form and in its modified form. To achieve our objective, we work with the curved DO in spherical coordinates, where we use the tetrad formalism. So, by defining a stationary ansatz for the spinor, we obtain two coupled first-order differential equations, and by substituting one equation into the other, we obtain a second-order differential equation. To analytically and exactly solve this differential equation, we use a change of function and of variable. From this, we obtain the well-known Whittaker equation, whose solution is the Whittaker function. Consequently, we obtain the energy spectrum, which is quantized in terms of the radial quantum number $n$ and the angular quantum number $κ$, and explicitly depends on the angular frequency $ω$ (describes the DO), curvature parameter $a$ (describes the cloud of strings), and on the effective rest mass $m_{\text{eff}}$ (describes the rest mass modified by the curvature of spacetime). Besides, we graphically analyze the behavior of the spectrum as a function of $ω$ and $a$ for three different values of $n$ and $κ$, as well as the behavior of the radial probability density for four different values of $κ$, $ω$, and $a$ (with $n=0$).

Abstract: We investigate the renormalization group flow of a gravity--matter system in which a scalar field is minimally coupled to Einstein gravity and its kinetic term is given by a scale-dependent form factor $f_Λ(-\Box)$. Employing the Wilsonian proper-time flow equation, we derive a closed integro-differential equation that encodes the dependence of the form factor on the UV cutoff $Λ$. We solve the resulting fixed-point problem with a pseudospectral discretization and find a non-trivial fixed point for which $f_\ast(-\Box)$ departs from the canonical $-\Box$ behavior. Linearizing the flow about this solution yields a discrete spectrum of perturbations and a corresponding set of critical exponents, indicating a non-trivial scaling structure in this non-local sector compatible with asymptotic safety. We also observe that the form factor becomes local once the UV cutoff is removed, suggesting that the bare action associated with this fixed point is local in the scalar two-point sector.

Abstract: We extend the worldline quantum field theory formalism to include a direct diagrammatic method of computing the total flux of angular momentum from a black hole scattering event in the post-Minkowskian regime. In the former case, topological solutions, such as the BTZ black hole, deficit angles, and naked singularities, emerge from identifying points in AdS using elements from its isometry algebra $so(2,2)$. The type of solution corresponds one-to-one with the orbits of $so(2,2)$. We demonstrate how various double copies of four-dimensional AdS gravity similarly arise from the $so(2,3)$ isometry elements, which also correspond one-to-one with their orbits through a Penrose-type transform. We classify all such elements and generate the corresponding double copies, which include AdS black holes, black branes, and many others. The double-copy isometries originate from the centralizer of a given AdS isometry, allowing us to define canonical coordinates associated with its Abelian part. Additionally, the two Casimir invariants of $so(2,3)$ feature in the metrics. Our classification naturally extends to higher spins, providing nonequivalent multicopies at the linearized level.

</details>

Method: 采用超几何（supergeometry）框架系统构建高形式对称性，定义并分析拓扑守恒超流，特别聚焦于Chern-Weil型及其几何推广形式；在三维N=1超麦克斯韦理论中具体实现算符构造与缺陷刻画，引入超链数（super-linking number）定义荷。

Conclusion: 超几何为系统研究超对称理论中高形式对称性提供了自然语言；Chern-Weil及其几何推广构成重要对称性源；super-symTFT可望成为连接超对称、拓扑场论与量子引力的关键桥梁。

Abstract: We review the construction of higher-form symmetries for supersymmetric theories using a supergeometry framework. This reveals an enlarged set of topological conserved supercurrents, including Chern-Weil symmetries and new geometric Chern-Weil symmetries built from invariant supermanifold forms. In N=1 super-Maxwell theory in three dimensions, we construct the corresponding operators and charged defects, with charges determined by a super-linking number between their supporting hypersurfaces. At the end we provide as an original unpublished contribution some hints on how to construct super-symTFT for Chern-Weil and geometric Chern-Weil symmetries directly from supergravity.

### [19] [On the Consistency of Null Strings Literature: The Tale of an Overlooked Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12414)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 零弦在 D 维时空中的物理传播自由度数为 D−3，而非此前公认的 D−2。

Conclusion: 以往零弦研究因忽略该局域对称性而存在系统性错误，所有相关结论均需重新审视与修正。

Abstract: We observe that the null string action possesses a previously overlooked local symmetry. By correctly accounting for this symmetry, we show that the number of physical propagating degrees of freedom of null strings in $D$ dimensional target space is $D-3$, in contrast to $D-2$ that one finds in the literature. Overlooking this symmetry has led to an unphysical over-counting of states, rendering the null string analyses inconsistent. Thus, our observation calls for a thorough revision of all statements and results in the null string literature.

### [20] [Non-vacuum gravitational effective action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12447)
*Andrei O. Barvinsky,Farahmand Hasanov,Nikita Kolganov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在准热力学框架下，针对非真空量子态的波算符，构建了热核迹与单圈有效作用量的曲率展开；该框架基于具有周期边界条件（周期β=1/T）的非静态、非定态欧氏引力背景，并通过度规引力势局部重标度T得到有效温度；结果在平直欧氏空间上的度规扰动二次近似下获得，并以时空曲率协变化表达，引入广义类时周期性条件下的矢量场ξ^μ(x)以推广静态几何中的Killing矢量；该矢量场导出局域Tolman温度形式T/√(ξ²(x))，并在高‘温度’渐近下获得了非局域形式因子的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为处理非真空量子态在非静态、非定态引力背景下的热力学性质，需推广传统静态/稳态下的Tolman温度与热核方法，建立适用于任意类时周期性度规的协变热核展开框架。

Method: 在平直欧氏空间上对度规做二次微扰，结合类时周期性边界条件（周期β=1/T），构造协变化的热核迹与单圈有效作用量曲率展开；引入满足协变定义的矢量场ξ^μ(x)作为Killing矢量的推广，并据此定义局域有效温度；推导高温度下非局域形式因子的渐近行为。

Result: 得到了热核迹与单圈有效作用量关于曲率的协变二次展开式；导出了广义局域温度T/√(ξ²(x))，在静态极限下退化为标准Tolman温度；获得了高温度下非局域形式因子的渐近结构；讨论了其在宇宙学中的潜在应用。

Conclusion: 该工作成功将热核方法与Tolman热力学推广至一般类时周期性但非稳态的引力背景，为研究早期宇宙、黑洞附近或强时变引力场中的量子效应提供了协变工具。

Abstract: Curvature expansion for the heat kernel trace and the one-loop effective action is built for the wave operator of the theory in the quasi-thermal setup of a nonvacuum quantum state. This setup implies a non-static and non-stationary Euclidean gravitational background with periodic boundary conditions of the period $β=1/T$, where $T$ plays the role of effective global temperature to be locally rescaled by the metric gravitational potential. The results are obtained in the approximation quadratic in metric perturbations on top of flat Euclidean space and covariantized in terms of spacetime curvature. Covariantization includes a special vector field $ξ^μ(x)$ which generalizes the Killing vector of static geometries with time translation isometry to the case of a generic arbitrarily inhomogeneous metric subject to timelike periodicity condition. This vector field is obtained as a covariant metric functional to quadratic order in metric perturbations and gives rise to the local function $T/\sqrt{ξ^2(x)}$, $ξ^2(x)=g_{μν}(x)ξ^μ(x)ξ^ν(x)$, reducing to Tolman temperature $T/\sqrt{g_{00}(x)}$ on stationary manifolds with Killing symmetry. High ``temperature'' asymptotic behavior of the nonlocal formfactors -- operator coefficients of the curvature tensor structures in the heat kernel and effective action -- are obtained and possible cosmological applications of these results are discussed.

### [22] [Cutting rules in strong field QED with application to trident pair production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12479)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 确立了两圈辐射修正与三叉过程速率之间的严格对应；给出了恒定交叉场中三叉过程速率的完整解析表达式（含自旋分辨的直接与交换项）；指出总产额可通过切割规则从高圈虚部可靠获得，但微分产额重建需谨慎；验证了切割规则在任意圈阶及非微扰背景下的适用性。

Conclusion: 切割规则是连接高阶QED修正与物理过程产额的有力工具，不仅适用于微扰圈图，还可拓展至强场非微扰区域；但将其用于微分观测量时需注意背景场导致的动量约束与相空间重构问题。

Abstract: Following Veltman's approach, we formulate and discuss a general cutting equation for QED in a plane-wave background. We apply the corresponding cutting rules to justify the connection between the two-loop radiative corrections to elastic electron scattering and the rate of the trident process in a constant crossed field. As a byproduct, we compare the previously published results for the trident process in a constant crossed field and present a complete analytical expression for direct and exchange contributions to its rate, which is resolved in the spin of the initial electron. Our findings establish that although total rates can be reliably extracted from higher-loop by applying the cutting rules, reconstruction of differential rates requires additional care. The cutting rules apply to any loop order and may be extended to nonperturbative regimes.

### [23] [Anomalies in Neural Network Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12488)
*Christian Ferko,Samuel Frank,James Halverson,Vishnu Jejjala*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出神经网络场论（NN-FT），将场论建模为网络架构及其参数分布，并推导出其Schwinger-Dyson方程与Ward恒等式，用于研究各类反常（如U(1)、尺度、Weyl反常及拓扑反常），所有结果均在参数空间中获得，提供理解量子场论对称性的新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建神经网络场论（NN-FT）形式体系，定义参数空间上的密度与守恒流；推导该框架下的Schwinger-Dyson方程和Ward恒等式；引入参数空间守恒流刻画对称性及其破缺；通过纤维平均等方式恢复局域性；将方法应用于前馈网络、注意力机制及多个物理模型（复标量U(1)、4D φ⁴尺度反常、弦论Weyl反常等）。

Result: 成功导出NN-FT中的Schwinger-Dyson方程与Ward恒等式；揭示参数空间守恒流对刻画对称性与反常的核心作用；给出Weyl反常下玻色弦临界维度的新计算；处理离散拓扑数据（如缠绕数、T对偶）的反常行为；证明该形式在非局域NN-FT中仍适用，并可退化至局域Lagrangian情形。

Conclusion: NN-FT为量子场论提供了基于神经网络参数空间的新表述，不仅拓展了反常理论的适用范围，也架起了机器学习架构与基础物理之间的概念桥梁；参数空间视角有望成为研究对称性与量子效应的普适新范式。

Abstract: Neural network field theory (NN-FT) formulates field theory in terms of a network architecture and a density on its parameters. We derive Schwinger--Dyson equations and Ward identities in NN-FT and utilize them to study anomalies. The equations depend on a conserved parameter space current that characterizes symmetries and how they break. It is relevant even in non-local NN-FTs, but can recover local currents in the case of a local Lagrangian by an appropriate fiber-wise average. In machine learning, this formalism is applied to feedforward networks and the attention mechanism. In physics, we use this machinery to study $U(1)$ symmetry for a complex scalar, the scale anomaly in $4d$ massless $φ^4$ theory, the Weyl anomaly for the bosonic string (including a new computation of the critical dimension), and examples involving discrete topological data, such as winding numbers and T-duality. Since the results are obtained in network parameter space rather than the standard field space, they represent a new way to understand symmetries in quantum field theories.

### [24] [Clustering constraints on super-early galaxy formation scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11064)
*Antonio Matteri,Andrea Pallottini,Andrea Ferrara*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文探讨了JWST发现的高红移（z≳10）明亮蓝星系丰度异常现象，系统比较了四种模型（无衰减、无反馈爆发、爆发式恒星形成、原初黑洞）对星系聚类性质（特别是偏置参数b）的预测差异，发现它们在较暗星系中偏置相似，但在较亮星系中显著分化；当前观测尚不足以区分模型，但未来更精确的JWST数据有望打破现有简并。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST观测到大量高红移（z≳10）明亮蓝星系，远超此前理论预期，亟需通过可观测的统计量（如星系聚类）来甄别不同物理起源模型。

Method: 基于Shin-Uchuu暗物质模拟，在z≈11时用四类典型模型（i) 无衰减、ii) 无反馈爆发、iii) 爆发式恒星形成、iv) 原初黑洞）赋予晕内星系，并计算不同UV星等限样本的两点相关函数和偏置参数b。

Result: 所有模型在M_UV≈−16时预测相似偏置（b≈7），但在M_UV≲−18时明显分化：原初黑洞模型给出近似与亮度无关的b，其余模型则显示b随亮度增强至≈14；当前观测精度尚无法显著排除任一模型。

Conclusion: 星系聚类（尤其是偏置参数随UV星等的变化关系b(M_UV)）是区分高红移星系形成物理机制的有力探针，但需更高精度的JWST观测和更完善的理论建模才能打破当前模型简并。

Abstract: The unexpectedly high abundance of bright, blue, super-early galaxies ($z\gtrsim10$) has challenged most pre-JWST models of early galaxy formation and motivated a wide range of proposed explanations. We systematically investigate whether galaxy clustering can discriminate among representative scenarios that reproduce the observed UV luminosity function. Using the Shin-Uchuu dark-matter-only simulation, we populate $z \approx 11$ halos with galaxies according to solutions based on i) attenuation-free, ii) feedback-free bursts, iii) bursty star formation, and iv) primordial black hole models. For each model, we compute the two-point correlation function and predict the galaxy bias for flux-limited samples at different thresholds in the $-20 < {\rm M_{UV}} < -16$ magnitude range. We find that all models predict similar bias values ($b \approx 7$) for faint galaxies (${\rm M_{UV}}\approx-16$), but diverge at ${\rm M_{UV}}\lesssim-18$, as the underlying halo-mass to ${\rm M_{UV}}$ relations differ significantly. In particular, the primordial black hole scenario predicts an almost luminosity-independent bias, whereas the other models generally predict increasing bias with luminosity, reaching $b \approx 14$ for ${\rm M_{UV}} \approx -19$. Current observational estimates of the bias cannot yet rule out any of the models at a significant statistical confidence. More precise measurements from future JWST programs, together with improved theoretical predictions, will be required to break the present degeneracies. Ideally, constraints from a complete sample of galaxies with ${\rm M_{UV}} < -18$ would probe the knee of the $b({\rm M_{UV}})$ function, taking advantage of the difference in model predictions and strengthening our analysis. Although requiring further refinement, galaxy clustering is confirmed to be a promising probe of the physical origin of the JWST high-redshift luminosity function.

</details>


### [25] [A correlation predicting galaxies without dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11070)
*Michal Bílek*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文研究了暗物质缺失星系的识别方法，发现其重子分数与重子引力加速度或面亮度存在强相关性，表明这些星系可能是标准形成过程在极端条件下的产物，而非奇异机制所致，并提出了一个基于面亮度的观测判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准星系形成理论预测所有星系都应含有暗物质，但近年发现的一些星系似乎缺乏暗物质，挑战了现有理论，因此需要探究是否能仅从重子性质识别这类星系。

Method: 利用超弥散星系和矮椭球星系样本，系统搜索基于恒星质量、有效半径、到宿主距离及宿主重子质量预测重子分数的经验公式，并分析其与重子引力加速度（a_bar）或平均面亮度的关系。

Result: 发现重子分数最强地依赖于a_bar（或等效的面亮度），呈近似a_bar^{-1}关系；已确认的暗物质缺失星系位于该关系的极端端；预测g波段面亮度亮于约25 mag arcsec^{-2}的超弥散星系应具有极低暗物质含量。

Conclusion: 暗物质缺失星系很可能是标准星系形成过程在异常强烈条件下产生的自然结果，而非需引入新物理机制；所发现的相关性提供了一个简单有效的观测筛选标准。

Abstract: The standard theory of galaxy formation predicts that all galaxies should contain dark matter, yet a handful of recently discovered galaxies appear to lack it, challenging our understanding of galaxy formation. We investigate whether such dark-matter deficient objects can be identified from their baryonic properties alone, analogously to the radial-acceleration relation, which tightly links baryon and dark matter distributions in spiral galaxies. Using a sample of ultra-diffuse and dwarf spheroidal galaxies -- systems whose baryonic properties resemble those of the confirmed dark-matter-deficient galaxies -- we systematically search for a formula to predict baryonic fractions from stellar mass, effective radius, distance to the host, and the host's baryonic mass. We find that baryonic fraction correlates most strongly with the gravitational acceleration expected from baryons alone, $a_\mathrm{bar}$, or equivalently, with mean surface brightness, following an approximately $a_\mathrm{bar}^{-1}$ dependence. This scaling resembles the radial-acceleration relation but differs in functional form and applies to a different galaxy population. Strikingly, the dark-matter-deficient galaxies occupy the extreme end of the correlation. This suggests that they result from standard formation processes operating at unusual intensities rather than from exotic mechanisms. Importantly, the correlation predicts that all ultra-diffuse galaxies brighter than approximately 25 mag arcsec$^{-2}$ in the $g$-band should have very low dark matter content, offering a straightforward observational criterion for identifying these rare objects.

</details>


### [26] [The $R$-Process Alliance: The $R$-Process Enhancement of Stars from Chemodynamically Tagged Groups in the Milky Way Halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11087)
*Jessica Merritt Agnos,Charli M. Sakari,Pedro Silva,Terese T. Hansen,Erika M. Holmbeck,Ian U. Roederer,Hal France,Truman Farr,Rana Ezzeddine,Anna Frebel,Vinicius M. Placco,Timothy C. Beers*

TL;DR: 本文基于高分辨率光谱分析，对三颗贫金属星进行了详细重元素丰度测量，确认其中两颗为r-II型星，一颗接近r-I型星，并通过钍放射性定年发现其r-过程物质年龄均超过100亿年，且未见锕系增强；结果支持它们可能源自被吸积进银河系晕的矮星系（如Thamnos结构），但彼此起源环境不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究r-过程增强贫金属星的化学丰度特征及其起源环境，特别是它们是否来自共同的矮星系遗迹（如Thamnos结构），以理解银河系早期化学演化与并合历史。

Method: 利用Magellan望远镜MIKE光谱仪获取的高分辨率（R~80,000）、高信噪比光谱，对三颗已知r-过程候选星进行细致的29种重元素丰度分析，并结合钍（Th）放射性定年法估算r-过程发生时间。

Result: 确认2MASS J14592981−3852558和J15211026−0607566为r-II星，J19445483−4039459略低于r-I阈值；r-II星显示裂变碎片轻微增强；两颗r-II星的r-过程物质年龄>10 Gyr，无锕系增强；三颗星丰度模式各异，不支持共同起源，但各自可与Thamnos原星系一致。

Conclusion: 这三颗星很可能分别形成于不同但类似的矮星系环境中（如Thamnos），后被银河系吸积；其r-过程事件古老且非锕系增强型，暗示早期宇宙中存在多种r-过程源或喷发条件差异。

Abstract: As part of the ongoing work of the $R$-Process Alliance (RPA), detailed abundance measurements of 29 heavy elements in three metal-poor stars, 2MASS J14592981$-$3852558, 2MASS J19445483$-$4039459, and 2MASS J15211026$-$0607566, are presented based on an analysis of high-resolution ($R\sim 80,000$), high signal-to-noise ``portrait'' spectra from the Magellan Inamori Kyocera Echelle (MIKE) spectrograph on the Magellan-Clay Telescope at Las Campanas Observatory. The selected targets were identified as $r$-process-enhanced metal-poor stars in previous RPA snapshot analyses. They have also been linked to possible chemodynamically tagged groups, indicating that the stars may have formed in dwarf galaxies that were later accreted into the Milky Way halo. These stars have also been tentatively linked to the Thamnos structure. The detailed chemical abundances in this work confirm that 2MASS J14592981$-$3852558 and J15211026$-$0607566 are $r$-II stars, while 2MASS J19445483$-$4039459 is found to lie just below the threshold for $r$-I status. The $r$-II stars show signs of slight enhancement in fission fragments compared to 2MASS J19445483$-$4039459. Based on radioactive age dating with Th, the $r$-process material in the two $r$-II stars is found to be old (with ages $>10$ Gyr); neither star shows signs of an actinide boost. The varying elemental compositions suggest that these stars likely did not originate in the same environment, though each could be consistent with originating in the Thamnos progenitor.

### [27] [Tracing Radio AGN-Driven Quenching in Post-Starburst Galaxies at Cosmic Noon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11101)
*Pallavi Patil,Kate Rowlands,Katherine Alatalo,Omar Almaini,Vivienne Wild,David Maltby,Rob J. Ivison,Vinod Arumugam,K. Decker French,Timothy Heckman,Mark Lacy,Yuanze Luo,Kristina Nyland,Justin Atsushi Otter,Andreea Petric,Namrata Roy,Maya Skarbinski*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究通过VLA 1.4 GHz射电观测，分析宇宙正午（0.5<z<3）光度选择的后星暴星系（PSBs），发现其射电探测率低（尤其对非大质量样本），但大质量PSBs中AGN活动迹象明显（射电光度远超恒星形成贡献、形态致密），暗示短时标、弱喷流型射电AGN反馈可能在星系演化后期起维护作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究射电波段活动星系核（AGN）是否与宇宙正午时期星系恒星形成熄灭过程相关。

Method: 利用UKIDSS UDS深场中光度选择的宇宙正午后星暴星系样本，与深度VLA 1.4 GHz射电成像数据交叉匹配；结合射电探测率统计、光度分析、形态分类及未探测样本堆叠分析。

Result: 大质量PSBs（M*>10^11 M⊙）射电探测率为5±2%，其射电光度（L_1.4 ~ 10^22.8–10^24.9 W/Hz）显著高于恒星形成预期（中位高出37倍），且形态致密（≤15 kpc），提示弱射电AGN；堆叠分析在最高质量组中给出3.9σ弱探测；相比而言，宁静星系射电探测率更高（8±1%）、更易呈现延展喷流结构。

Conclusion: PSBs中射电AGN处于短占空比、弱喷流状态，支持其在星系演化后期以‘维持模式’反馈抑制恒星再生，而非主导早期快速熄灭。

Abstract: We present a radio continuum study of photometrically selected cosmic noon (0.5<z<3) post-starburst galaxies (PSBs) in the UKIDSS Deep Survey (UDS) field to assess if radio-mode Active Galactic Nuclei (AGN) are linked to the quenching of star formation at cosmic noon. Our cross-matching using the deep Very Large Array (VLA) imaging at 1.4 GHz results in a mean radio detection fraction ($f_{det}$) of only 0.8$\%$ for PSBs above a radio luminosity threshold of $L_{\rm 1.4 GHz} \geq 10^{24}$ W Hz$^{-1}$, increasing to 5$\pm2\%$ for massive PSBs with stellar masses M$_*>10^{11}$M$_\odot$. Massive PSBs have a comparable detection fraction to that of massive quiescent galaxies ($f_{det}=8\pm1\%$), and both classes have lower fractions than that of massive star-forming galaxies ($f_{det}=13\pm1\%$) in the same field. The radio luminosities of detected PSBs, ${\rm L}_{1.4}\sim 10^{22.8}-10^{24.9}$W/Hz, exceed those from star formation by a median factor of 37 indicative of a possible AGN origin. Their compact morphologies ($\lesssim15$ kpc at $z_{med}=1.5$) suggest low-luminosity AGN with less powerful jets. Stacking the undetected PSBs reveals a weak radio detection ($3.9σ$) in the highest mass bin (M$_*>10^{11}$M$_\odot$). In contrast, 1.4 GHz detected quiescent galaxies have radio luminosities reaching radio-loud levels, and a higher prevalence of extended morphologies indicative of large-scale jetted AGN. The AGN contribution is also detected in stacked measurements of quiescent galaxies. Overall, our results support a short radio AGN duty cycle for PSBs, characterized by weak radio jets, suggesting radio-driven maintenance mode feedback may become important at older ages.

Abstract: An update of the evidence that radio galaxies and clusters of galaxies are more common than average near the plane of the de Vaucouleurs Local Supercluster shows that in the distance range 100 to 200Mpc objects whose positions are correlated with the plane of the Local Supercluster include galaxies that are exceptionally luminous at two microns, radio galaxies, and clusters of galaxies. There can be little doubt about this property of cosmic structure. I also argue for detection of this correlation for the galaxies at 400Mpc distance that are exceptionally luminous at two microns. It will be interesting to learn whether these results are expected in the standard cosmology.

### [29] [The applicability of the JAGB method for measuring the distance of galaxies subject to different metal enrichment rates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11198)
*Claudio Gavetti,Paolo Ventura,Flavia Dell'Agli,Luca Graziani,Matteo Correnti,Chiara Ventura,Fabio La Franca*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析研究了JAGB方法在星系距离测量中的稳健性，发现J波段平均星等MavJ对星系演化历史不敏感，是更可靠的测距指标，其值为-6.2±0.05 mag；而J波段光度函数峰值位置则受金属增丰历史显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JAGB方法作为本地星系群及更远星系的距离指示器虽被提出，但其适用条件及J区域恒星的本质尚不明确，需厘清其对宿主星系演化历史（尤其是金属增丰历史）的依赖性。

Method: 采用基于AGB恒星演化模型与尘埃形成过程耦合的星族合成方法，构建不同星际介质金属增丰历史假设下的(J-Ks, J)色-星等图及相应J波段光度函数（JLF），分析JLF对金属增丰效率的依赖性。

Result: JAGB恒星主要形成于约1–6 Gyr前；JLF形状和峰值位置（变化超0.3 mag）强烈依赖金属增丰历史；而J波段平均星等MavJ几乎不受影响，恒为-6.2±0.05 mag；同时讨论了红巨星支阶段质量损失过程不确定性带来的影响。

Conclusion: MavJ比JLF峰值更适合作为JAGB距离指示器，因其对星系演化历史鲁棒性强；该结果提升了JAGB方法在星系距离测量中的可靠性，但也提示需进一步约束低质量恒星的质量损失物理。

Abstract: The JAGB method has been proposed in recent years as a possible distance indicator for galaxies in the Local Group and beyond. However, the nature of the stars populating the J region, and the conditions required for the direct application of this method, still need to be clarified. We investigate the robustness of the JAGB method through a detailed theoretical analysis of the stars populating the J region of the (J-Ks, J) diagram. The main goal is to identify the properties of the corresponding J luminosity function (JLF) that are minimally affected by the previous evolutionary history of the host galaxy, particularly its metal enrichment history. We use a population synthesis approach based on AGB stellar evolution models coupled consistently with dust formation in the stellar wind. Synthetic stellar distributions in the (J-Ks, J) diagram and the related JLFs are calculated for different assumptions on the metallicity evolution of the interstellar medium, in order to study how the JLF depends on the efficiency of metal enrichment. We find that the JAGB population is dominated by stars formed between about 1 and 6 Gyr ago, while stars formed outside this interval contribute only marginally to the JAGB region. The shape of the JLF strongly depends on the metal enrichment history, and the position of the J-band peak varies by more than 0.3 mag among the different cases explored. Conversely, the mean J-band magnitude, MavJ, is much less sensitive to the previous history of the galaxy and therefore represents a more reliable distance indicator. For all the cases investigated we find MavJ = -6.2 +/- 0.05 mag. We also discuss the uncertainties related to the still poorly constrained mass-loss process experienced by low-mass stars during the red giant branch phase.

### [30] [Variable stars in the field of the Galactic globular cluster M71](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11227)
*C. C. Cortés,D. Deras,A. Arellano Ferro,S. Muneer,I. H. Bustos Fierro*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: M71 is a nearby, metal-rich globular cluster at low Galactic latitude, where field contamination and spatially variable extinction complicate colour-magnitude diagrams (CMDs) and the identification of cluster member variable stars. Our aims are (i) to construct a homogeneous census of variable stars in M71 by refining their periods and classifications and identifying new candidates, and (ii) to derive a decontaminated, differentially dereddened CMD to constrain its physical properties. We obtained Johnson-Kron-Cousins $VI$ time-series CCD photometry and reduced it using difference image analysis. Cluster membership was established from \textit{Gaia}~DR3 proper motions, and a differential-reddening correction was applied across the field of view. The resulting CMD, cleaned of field stars, was compared with tailored isochrones to estimate age ($12.9^{+0.9}_{-0.8}$ Gyr), metallicity ([Fe/H] =$-0.88^{+0.13}_{-0.15}$), mean reddening ($E(B-V)$ = $0.21 \pm 0.02$), and distance modulus ($(m-M)_{0}$ = $13.01 \pm 0.06$). Variable stars were identified using two complementary approaches: a periodogram-free string-length scan refined with phase dispersion minimisation, and a robust inter-site screening based on median statistics combined with a generalised Lomb-Scargle significance criterion. We identified 21 variable stars not previously reported in the Catalog of Variable Stars in Globular Clusters and provided their periods, amplitudes, classifications, membership status, and light curves. This combined strategy yields a consistent picture of M71, expanding its known variable-star population and confirming parameters typical of metal-rich Galactic disk globular clusters.

### [31] [The Internal Nebular Attenuation Curve of Three-Dimensional Turbulent HII regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11377)
*Yifei Jin,Yong Shi,Ralph Sutherland,Ziyu Huang,Chuanfei Dong*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过在M3D代码中实现尘埃蒙特卡洛辐射转移，研究了Hii区内部湍流尘埃遮蔽对氢发射线的影响，发现其导致Hα/Hβ比值偏离标准Case B值（约3.02–3.03 vs. 2.86），源于较冷（<10,000 K）且密度/温度起伏的电离气体，并表明团块结构不改变内禀消光曲线斜率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hii区内部尘埃衰减会削弱观测到的发射线流量，而其中湍流密度场导致视线方向遮蔽程度变化，影响标准发射线比值（如Hα/Hβ）的可靠性，需更真实的辐射转移建模。

Method: 在最新M3D代码中嵌入尘埃蒙特卡洛辐射转移模块，生成不同马赫数下受内部湍流尘埃遮蔽影响的发射线图像；结合Hii区密度与温度涨落，模拟氢线辐射转移，计算Hα/Hβ比值及内禀消光曲线。

Result: Hα/Hβ比值为3.02–3.03，显著高于Case B理论值2.86，归因于Hii区温度低于10,000 K；推导出的内禀消光曲线斜率不受团块结构影响，因致密团块的强遮蔽被局地增强的发射强度所补偿。

Conclusion: 标准Case B假设在真实湍流Hii区中不成立；内禀消光曲线形状稳健，但发射线比值需考虑热力学与湍流结构联合效应；该工作为星系光谱诊断和尘埃校正提供更物理的基准。

Abstract: The internal dust attenuation of the Hii region reduces the observed emission-line fluxes. Turbulent density fields within each Hii region change the degree of the line-of-the-sight obscuration of the emission-line fluxes. In this paper, we implement the dust Monte-Carlo radiative transfer in the latest M3D code, creating the emission-line maps attenuated by the internal turbulent dust obscuration with the varying Mach numbers. The internal density and temperature fluctuations of Hii regions make the radiative transfer of hydrogen lines neither Case A nor Case B conditions, resulting in the global Hα to H\b{eta} ratio of approximately 3.02-3.03, differing from the widely-used value of 2.86. This deviation from Case B is because the temperature of these Hii regions is cooler than 10,000 K. We further derive the internal nebular attenuation curve from the attenuated Hydrogen lines, finding that the clumpy structures within Hii regions do not change the slope of the internal attenuation curve. This is because the heavy dust obscuration of dense clumps is canceled out by the high in-situ production of emission-line intensities.

### [32] [Exploring the stellar streams and satellites around the giant low surface brightness galaxy Malin 1](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11419)
*Roy O. E. Bustos-Espinoza,Matias Blaña,Gaspar Galaz,Marcelo D. Mora,Junais,Mousumi Das,Sudhanshu Barway,Ankit Kumar,Evelyn J. Johnston,Thomas Puzia*

TL;DR: 本文通过构建Malin 1的引力势模型（含恒星、气体与暗物质成分），结合NFW和ISO两种暗晕轮廓，研究其卫星星系轨道动力学及其与两条巨型恒星流的关联；结果表明部分卫星轨道为束缚态，其潮汐作用可解释恒星流结构，支持卫星相互作用塑造gLSBG形态的观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于光学与HI观测数据构建包含恒星、气体及暗物质组分的引力势模型；在宽参数空间内测试NFW与ISO两种暗晕分布假设；通过轨道积分模拟卫星运动轨迹，并比对其与恒星流的空间/运动学一致性。

Result: ISO暗晕模型（M_vir ≈ 2.6×10¹² M⊙）比NFW模型（M_vir ≈ 1.4×10¹² M⊙）更易产生束缚卫星轨道；最远卫星约1.6 Gyr前到达近心点，较近伴星则早在~100 Myr前发生相互作用；某近邻伴星在径向与极向轨道上均呈现领头与拖尾星流特征；同时发现若干非束缚解亦能连接卫星与星流。

Conclusion: 卫星与恒星流的空间-运动学对齐表明Malin 1当前形态主要由过去卫星相互作用塑造；轨道建模有效约束了可能的前身天体及其轨道历史，为理解gLSBG的动力学演化提供了关键依据；结果与近期基于Malin 1运动学数据的研究一致。

Abstract: Context. Giant Low Surface Brightness galaxies, such as Malin 1, host extended discs exceeding 100 kpc. Their formation and evolution remain debated, with interactions with satellite galaxies and accretion streams proposed as key contributors. Malin 1 hosts satellites and exhibits two giant stellar streams, likely the result of past interactions. Aims. We investigate the orbital dynamics of Malin 1's satellites and their possible connections with observed stellar streams, testing their nature with different formation scenarios. Methods. We constructed gravitational potentials using optical and HI data, including stellar, gaseous, and dark matter components, and explored a wide parameter space while testing NFW and ISO halo profiles. Results. Some scenarios produced bound solutions. The ISO halo model ($M_{\text{Virial}} \approx 2.6 \times 10^{12}~M_{\odot}$) favours bound satellite orbits more than the NFW model ($M_{\text{Virial}} \approx 1.4 \times 10^{12}~M_{\odot}$). Giant stellar streams could be substructures of some satellite galaxies along their leading and trailing trajectories. The most distant Malin 1 satellite could have reached pericenter $\sim 1.6$ Gyr ago, while closer companions interacted as early as $\sim 100$ Myr ago. At the same time, one close companion displays both leading and trailing arms in radial and polar orbits. Furthermore, we also identify some unbound solutions linking satellites with streams. Conclusions. Satellites and stream alignment indicate that past interactions shaped Malin 1's morphology. Our modelling constrains progenitors and orbital histories, providing insights into the dynamical evolution of gLSBGs. Findings are consistent with recent studies using Malin 1 kinematic data.

### [33] [Metal Enrichment by the First Stars Exploding at the Lower Energy Limit of Pair-Instability Supernovae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11647)
*Aron Kordt,Simon C. O. Glover,Ralf S. Klessen*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过宇宙学流体动力学模拟研究了低质量对不稳定超新星（PISN，140 M⊙，5×10⁵¹ erg）对第二代恒星金属增丰的影响，发现其产生的第二代恒星中位[Fe/H] ≈ −5.5，显著低于高能PISN情形；结果表明若PISN普遍发生，应在观测到的极贫金属星（EMP）中看到其特征奇偶丰度模式，而实际未观测到，因此PISN不太可能是早期金属增丰的主要机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释为何在本地极贫金属星（EMP）中未观测到对不稳定超新星（PISN）的特征丰度印记：是PISN本身稀有，还是其增丰后的第二代恒星金属丰度过高而无法落入EMP样本？此前工作聚焦高能PISN（270 M⊙, 10⁵³ erg），本文则补全低能端（140 M⊙, 5×10⁵¹ erg）情形。

Method: 采用自洽的宇宙学流体动力学模拟，追踪第三星族（Pop III）恒星形成、辐射与机械反馈，以及金属增丰气体中第二代恒星的形成；特别关注低质量PISN（140 M⊙，爆炸能5×10⁵¹ erg）的增丰效应，并分析第二代恒星的丰度模式与金属丰度分布。

Result: 所有第二代恒星均由同一晕内前身Pop III恒星内部增丰而成，呈现单颗第一代恒星的丰度特征；其中位[Fe/H] ≈ −5.5，比高能PISN情形低2.9 dex；该丰度仍处于EMP星典型范围（[Fe/H] < −3），理论上应可观测到PISN特有的奇偶元素丰度模式。

Conclusion: 若Pop III PISN普遍存在，则其特征丰度模式应在当前EMP星样本中被探测到；但实际未观测到，因此PISN作为早期金属增丰主导机制的可能性被强烈排除。

Abstract: The first generation of stars, Population III (Pop III), is believed to be massive, with some potentially having masses in the range 140 M$_\odot$ to 270 M$_\odot$ and capable of exploding as a pair-instability supernova (PISN). Such events release large amounts of energy and produce substantial quantities of metals, suggesting that they should leave characteristic signatures in the abundance patterns of extremely metal-poor (EMP) stars observed in the local Universe. No clear imprint of PISNe is seen in the local EMP star population, implying either that these events were rare or that stars forming from PISN-enriched gas had metallicities too high to find them in the EMP population. Previous work explored the latter possibility by investigating the enrichment by PISNe with masses and explosion energies at the upper end of the theoretical range (270 M$_\odot$, $10^{53}$ erg). Here, we complement that work at the opposite extreme: Pop III stars at the lower mass (140 M$_\odot$) and explosion energy ($5\cdot 10^{51}$ erg) limit. Using a cosmological hydrodynamic simulation, we self-consistently track the formation of Pop III stars, their radiative and mechanical feedback, and the subsequent formation of second-generation stars in metal-enriched gas. We find that all second-generation stars are exclusively internally enriched by their progenitor within the same halo, thereby imprinting the abundance pattern of a single first-generation star. The median [Fe/H] abundance of second-generation stars is ~ -5.5 which is 2.9 dex smaller than in the high-energy PISN case. Our results demonstrate that if Pop III PISNe were common, we would expect to find stars with the characteristic odd-even abundance pattern produced by PISNe within the observed EMP population. Their absence in observations therefore strongly disfavours PISNe as the dominant channel of early metal enrichment.

</details>


### [34] [Non-LTE atmosphere models of very luminous sources and their applicability to Little Red Dots, quasi-stars, and similar objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12141)
*Fabrice Martins,Daniel Schaerer,Rui Marques-Chaves*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文使用CMFGEN代码构建大质量恒星风大气模型，尝试解释‘小红点’（LRDs）的观测光谱特征；模型能较好再现多数LRD的SED、巴尔末减幅及金属发射线，但难以同时产生真实巴尔末跳变和强发射线，其物理解释能力仍存疑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究传统用于大质量恒星强风的大气模型是否能生成与‘小红点’（LRDs）观测光谱形态相似的合成光谱。

Method: 采用CMFGEN代码构建球对称、非LTE、膨胀大气模型，内边界辐射场热化并设温度为5000–12000 K，光度取1e10 Lsun，考虑多种金属丰度，并引入Av~1.9–2.7的尘埃消光。

Result: 模型成功再现LRDs的蓝光学连续谱、宽氢发射线（电子散射致宽）、近巴尔末/帕邢极限的连续SED、FeII/O/Ca等金属线，以及OI 8446 Å和1.129 μm荧光发射线；在适当消光下，红外再辐射能量也符合观测约束；但无法同时满足真实巴尔末跳变与强发射线。

Conclusion: CMFGEN大气模型可解释LRDs众多光谱特征，但内在物理条件（如是否存在真正巴尔末跳变）仍不明确，尚不能确定其相较于其他模型（如活动星系核或原初星系模型）更具优势。

Abstract: We investigate whether atmosphere models traditionally used for massive stars with strong winds can produce synthetic spectra morphologically similar to those of Little Red Dots (LRDs). We compute atmosphere models and synthetic spectra with the code CMFGEN. The models assume a thermalized radiation field at the inner boundary, parameterized by a temperature varying between 5000 and 12000~K. We adopt a typical luminosity of 1e10 Lsun. The models are spherical, assume an expanding atmosphere, and are computed under non-LTE conditions and for several metallicities. The spectral energy distribution (SED) is different from a blackbody, with a blue optical spectrum. Broad hydrogen emission lines are produced, their wings being formed by electron scattering. The SED near the Balmer and Paschen limit is rather continuous. A Balmer break is predicted for the coolest temperature models provided the wind density is reduced. The SED and Balmer decrement of most LRDs is reproduced by the models, provided they are dust-attenuated with Av~1.9-2.7. Assuming the absorbed luminosity is re-radiated in the infrared, the energy output at these wavelengths is consistent with observational constraints. The models predict FeII, oxygen and calcium lines. OI lines at 8446 A and 1.129 um are produced mostly by Lybeta fluorescence. The strength of emission lines from metals depends on input temperature, metallicity, and details of the radiative transfer models. CMFGEN atmosphere models predict a large number of spectral properties observed in many LRDs. They struggle to simultaneously produce a genuine Balmer break and strong emission lines. Whether they are more relevant or not to explain LRDs' spectra compared to alternative models is unclear, leaving open the question of the physical conditions in LRDs.

</details>


### [35] [Proximate damped Lyman-$α$ systems as tracers of quasar feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12188)
*Patrick Petitjean*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了近邻阻尼莱曼α吸收体（PDLAs）的起源，利用SDSS DR16数据识别并分类多种近邻吸收系统（ProxSys），发现不同类别构成连续物理序列，其激发态吸收、金属线强度和尘埃含量递减，并呈现多成分运动学特征；结果支持冷致密云在类星体附近参与进出流动的动态循环，与混沌冷吸积模型一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解活动星系核（AGN）反馈对宿主星系星际介质的影响至关重要，而近邻阻尼莱曼α吸收体（PDLAs）是探测该反馈中冷气体的关键探针，但其物理起源尚不清晰，需统一框架解释其多样性和动力学特征。

Method: 基于SDSS DR16数据库搜索类星体红移处的低电离金属吸收线系统（ProxSys），依据Lyman-α吸收强度、部分遮蔽特征及激发态谱线（如SiII*）对ProxSys进行分类（Ghostly、DLA-Cor、标准DLA、sub-DLA等），并分析其吸收强度序列、速度分布及中值叠加谱。

Result: 约13%的ProxSys属于Ghostly或DLA-Cor类，具强激发态吸收；各类别构成连续序列，SiII*、CIV、NV吸收强度与尘埃含量递减；标准DLA集中在±1000 km/s内（宿主星系气体），Ghostly/SiII*系统速度范围更广（-2000至+1200 km/s），含外流与少量内流成分；中值谱证实Ghostly和DLA-Cor起源于致密、部分遮蔽类星体发射区的气体。

Conclusion: 冷致密气体云在类星体近域参与动态进出流动循环，支持混沌冷吸积模型，为AGN反馈驱动星系演化提供了关键观测证据。

Abstract: Active galactic nuclei (AGN) profoundly affect the interstellar medium of their host galaxies through intense radiation fields and powerful winds. Characterising this feedback is essential for understanding galaxy formation and evolution. Here we revisit the origin of proximate damped Lyman-$α$ absorbers (PDLAs), which trace cold gas within 3000 km/s of the quasar redshift, and interpret their kinematics and physical properties within a unified framework. We searched the SDSS DR16 database for low-ionisation metal absorption-line systems at the quasar redshift (referred to as ProxSys). This approach enables us to identify and classify different types of proximate absorbers, including so-called Ghostly systems, coronagraphic DLAs (DLA-Cor), standard DLAs, and sub-DLAs, based on the presence of strong Lyman-alpha absorption, partial covering signatures, or excited atomic transitions such as SiII*. We find that about 13% of ProxSys belong to the Ghostly or DLA-Cor classes and exhibit strong absorption from excited species. The different classes of ProxSys form a continuous sequence characterised by decreasing SiII*, CIV, and NV absorption strengths and dust content. Their velocity distributions reveal multiple kinematic components. Standard DLAs cluster within 1000km/s of the quasar systemic redshift, consistent with gas in the host galaxy, whereas Ghostly and SiII* bearing systems display broader distributions, including outflows reaching -2000 km/s and a smaller population of inflowing clouds up to +1200 km/s. Median stacked spectra confirm that Ghostly and coronagraphic systems arise in dense, compact gas partially covering the quasar emission regions. These results support a scenario in which cold, dense clouds participate in a dynamic cycle of inflow and outflow in the vicinity of quasars, consistent with chaotic cold accretion.

### [36] [A tool of Hierarchical cOre ideNtification and Kinematic property AssIgnment (HONKAI) for Dense Cores](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12222)
*Jiawei Liu,Zhiyuan Ren,Di Li,Jinjin Xie,Gary A. Fuller,Yuchen Xing,Xin Lyu,Fengwei Xu,Chen Wang,Fanyi Meng,Sihan Jiao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IRDCs是大质量恒星和星团形成的最早期场所，解析其内部等级结构是基础且关键的任务，但现有方法多聚焦于数据处理的单一步骤，缺乏端到端的自动化流程。

Method: 开发了HONKAI（Hierarchical cOre ideNtification and Kinematic property AssIgnment）流程，实现多波段（850 μm尘埃连续谱与^{13}CO(1-0)谱线）数据中核与团块的自动识别、速度成分分解、物理性质测量及星表生成。

Result: 在三个IRDC中识别出193个致密核（分布在16个团块中）；其中136个核具有高维里比（R_vir > 1），但其质量-尺度关系低于大质量恒星形成阈值；核心质量函数（CMF）在高质量端斜率更陡，不同于演化更成熟的样本。

Conclusion: 多数IRDC致密核虽具自引力，但当前状态尚不足以直接形成大质量恒星；大质量恒星形成可能依赖后续的质量吸积或聚集过程。

Abstract: Infrared dark clouds (IRDCs) contains cold dense gas at the earliest stage of massive star and cluster formation. In studying the IRDCs, a universal and fundamental task is to resolve their internal hierarchical structures. Various packages and algorithms were developed for this purpose, but with most of them mainly focused on certain individual steps in data processing. In this work, we build a more automatic procedure for multi-band structure measurement HONKAI (Hierarchical cOre ideNtification and Kinematic property AssIgnment), which can resolve the elemental components including cores and clumps, disentangle the velocity components in spectral data, measure their physical properties, and generate a catalogue for all the measured properties. We use {\sc honkai} for a joint study towards three IRDCs observed in 850 $μ$m dust continuum with James Clerk Maxwell Telescope (JCMT) and the $^{13}CO$ $(1-0)$ data cube with the Purple Mount Observatory 14-m telescope. 193 dense cores in 16 clumps are identified. As major dynamical properties, a large amount of the cores (136 out of 193) are measured to have large virial ratio of $R_{\rm vir}>1$, but their mass-size relation is bellow the threshold for massive star formation. Meanwhile, core mass function (CMF) also exhibits a steeper slope towards high-mass end compared to more evolved core samples. These three properties in accordance suggest that although many IRDC cores are self-gravitating, only a small fraction are seemingly possible to form high-mass stars. In subsequent core evolution, some further mass assembly trend may be involved to facilitate the high-mass star formation.

### [37] [Self-consistent dynamical modelling of the Milky Way bar with orbital frequency analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12424)
*Zachary Langford,Robyn Sanderson,Madeline Lucey,Jason A. S. Hunt*

TL;DR: 本文更新了银河系棒状结构的频率分析方法，通过计算N体模拟势场中轨道的基本频率，识别支持棒结构的‘Warm’内林德布拉德共振（ILR）轨道，并结合Gaia、APOGEE和OGLE观测数据约束银河系棒的长度与模式速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为更精确测量银河系棒的物理性质（如长度和模式速度），需改进现有频率分析法对关键支持轨道（特别是贡献径向延伸的Warm ILR轨道）的识别能力。

Method: 更新轨道分类标准以专门识别‘Warm’内林德布拉德共振（ILR）轨道；在旋转的N体导出势模型中计算恒星轨道基本频率；将恒星归类为棒支持轨道成员；分析其近心点/远心点分布以确定棒的径向范围；应用Gaia、APOGEE和OGLE超过20万颗恒星的数据进行实证分析。

Result: 多个棒长度和模式速度组合与观测数据在5%误差范围内一致，表明当前数据尚不足以唯一确定银河系棒的具体参数。

Conclusion: 更新后的频率分析法能更有效地刻画棒结构的动力学基础，但需更高精度或更多维相空间数据才能进一步收窄银河系棒参数的不确定性。

Abstract: We present an update to the frequency analysis method for measuring the properties of a galactic bar. The method involves computing the fundamental frequencies of orbits in rotating, N-body-derived potential models, classifying the stars as members of bar supporting orbits, and finding the extent of the apo-centre distribution. In this work, we apply an updated classification criterion designed to isolate the so-called "Warm" inner Lindblad resonance (ILR) orbits. These orbits have been shown to contain the looped x1 orbits, which dominate the "shoulder regions" of the bar and largely contribute to the radial extent. We apply this method to existing Gaia, APOGEE, and OGLE data of more than 200,000 stars to constrain the properties of the Milky Way bar. We find that multiple bar lengths and pattern speeds are consistent with the data to within 5 percent.

### [38] [Photometric determination of the mass accretion rates of pre-main sequence stars. IX. Recent star formation in the periphery of NGC 346](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12486)
*Christiaan Dik,Guido De Marchi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文研究了SMC中NGC 346星团外围宁静区域的恒星形成性质和年轻恒星特征，利用哈勃望远镜多波段观测识别出137颗具有Hα超量的原恒星（PMS），测定了其物理参数，并发现其吸积率受邻近大质量恒星紫外辐射影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究宁静、低密度星形成区中恒星形成过程与环境（如大质量恒星辐射）的关系，补充对非典型星团环境下的恒星形成认知。

Method: 基于哈勃空间望远镜V、I及Hα窄带成像数据，结合等龄线拟合确定恒星年龄；通过Hα超量（5σ显著性、EW > 20 Å）识别原恒星候选体，并估算质量、年龄、吸积光度与吸积率；结合JWST近红外数据检验红外超量。

Result: 识别出137颗可靠PMS候选体，平均年龄~16 Myr、质量0.80±0.16 M⊙，中位吸积率为8.0×10⁻⁹ M⊙/yr；吸积状态及吸积率随距大质量星团距离增加而上升；部分PMS星在JWST波段显示近红外超量。

Conclusion: 即使在无明显星团和云气的宁静区域，仍存在持续的低效恒星形成活动；邻近大质量恒星的紫外辐射可能通过光致蒸发抑制附近PMS星的盘吸积，表明辐射反馈在低密度环境中亦起重要作用。

Abstract: We studied the properties of star formation and the characteristics of young stars in a quiet region located beyond the outskirts of the prominent star-forming cluster NGC 346 in the Small Magellanic Cloud (SMC). Utilising observations from the Hubble Space Telescope across the broad V and I bands, as well as the narrow Halpha band, we identified populations with ages of roughly 10, 60, 400 Myr and of 5 Gyr through isochrone comparison. We successfully identified 137 bona fide pre-main sequence (PMS) candidates exhibiting Halpha excess with a significance level of 5 sigma, accompanied by an Halpha line emission equivalent width exceeding 20 Å. Physical parameters for these PMS stars were determined, including mass, age, accretion luminosity, and mass accretion rate. Most PMS stars have an age around 16 Myr and an average mass of 0.80 \pm 0.16 M_sun. The median mass accretion rate for all 137 PMS stars is estimated to be about 8.0 x 10^(-9) M_sun/yr. While this rate is lower than that observed in the NGC 346 cluster itself, it is comparable with those measured for PMS stars in low-density star-forming regions in the SMC, despite the absence of apparent clustering and nebulosity. Furthermore, our analysis reveals that the ratios of accreting and non-accreting PMS stars to non-PMS stars and their mass accretion rate correlate with their distance from a group of hot massive stars in the vicinity. This suggests that the ultraviolet radiation emitted by these massive stars might erode the circumstellar discs of nearby PMS stars. Lastly, the overlap between our studied region and observations from the James Webb Space Telescope reveals that some of the identified PMS stars display near-infrared excess.

### [39] [Unveiling Hidden Lyman Alpha Emitters in the DESI DR1 Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12503)
*Jui-Kuan Chan,Ting-Wen Lan,J. Xavier Prochaska,Shun Saito,J. Aguilar,S. Ahlen,D. Bianchi,D. Brooks,A. Cuceu,A. de la Macorra,Biprateep Dey,P. Doel,A. Font-Ribera,J. E. Forero-Romero,E. Gaztañaga,Satya Gontcho A Gontcho,G. Gutierrez,C. Hahn,J. Jimenez,R. Joyce,S. Juneau,D. Kirkby,A. Kremin,M. Landriau,M. Manera,A. Meisner,R. Miquel,J. Moustakas,S. Nadathur,W. J. Percival,C. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前DESI处理流程无法有效识别和测量z>2星系的红移，导致大量Lyman alpha发射体（LAEs）被遗漏或红移估计错误，亟需专用方法挖掘这些高红移源。

Method: 基于人工目视检查构建包含LAEs与非LAEs的训练/测试样本，设计并训练CNN模型，实现LAE检测与Lyα红移测定双重任务。

Result: 模型达到95.2%纯度与95.9%完备率；在约200万条光谱中12分钟内检测出19685个z~2–3.5的LAEs；其复合光谱显示P-Cygni轮廓、MgII发射等关键特征，且多位于Lyα光度函数亮端（L_Lyα ≳ 10^43 erg/s）。

Abstract: We present an automatic method based on machine-learning convolutional neural network (CNN) architecture to detect Lyman alpha emitters (LAE) hidden in the Data Release 1 spectroscopic dataset of the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI). Those LAEs mostly have incorrect redshift estimations because the current DESI pipeline is not designed to detect and measure the redshifts of galaxies at $z>2$. To uncover those sources, we first visually inspect thousands of DESI spectra and construct a sample, consisting of both LAEs and non-LAEs, for training and testing the CNN-based model to (1) detect LAEs in DESI spectra and (2) determine their Ly$α$ redshifts. The final model yields $95.2\%$ purity and $95.9\%$ completeness for detecting LAEs. We apply this model to approximately $2\times10^{6}$ spectra of sources targeted as emission-line galaxies and detect 19,685 LAEs from $z\sim2$ to $3.5$ within 12 minutes with a single GPU, illustrating the high efficiency of this model for identifying LAEs. The detected LAEs are mostly at the bright end of the luminosity function with Ly$α$ luminosity $L_{\rm Lyα} \gtrsim 10^{43}$ erg/s. The high signal-to-noise composite spectrum of the detected LAEs further shows various spectral features, including P-Cygni profiles of metal lines and MgII emission lines, possible indicators of Lyman continuum escape fraction, revealing the rich astrophysical information in this LAE sample. Finally, this sample can be used to train and validate the pipelines for redshift determination of LAEs for the preparation of the DESI-II survey.

</details>

### [40] [The Impact of Cosmic Variance and Satellites on JWST Clustering Measurements at Redshift around 6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11077)
*Jiamu Huang,Elia Pizzati,Joseph F. Hennawi,Joop Schaye,Matthieu Schaller,Benjamin Snyder,Yi Kang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于JWST/NIRCam WFSS观测和FLAMINGO-10k模拟的贝叶斯框架，用于从z≈6的类星体与[O III]星系的成团性测量中推断其暗物质晕质量，并指出常用泊松误差严重低估真实不确定性，尤其忽略宇宙方差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高红移（z≈6）类星体和发射线星系的成团性分析中，传统泊松误差低估了真实测量误差，尤其忽略了宇宙方差和bin间相关性，导致晕质量等物理量推断不可靠。

Method: 基于FLAMINGO-10k N体模拟构建匹配ASPIRE巡天选择函数、视场与灵敏度的类星体与[O III]星系模拟样本；计算交叉与自相关函数及其包含宇宙方差和bin间相关的协方差矩阵（来自1000次实现）；采用贝叶斯方法拟合相关函数并推断最小晕质量。

Result: 1）泊松误差低估相关函数不确定性约3倍；2）使用泊松误差会低估推断的类星体与星系最小晕质量不确定性1.5–3倍；3）类星体晕质量推断对中心与卫星[O III]星系是否共享质量阈值不敏感。

Conclusion: 本文框架提供了更完备的误差预算，显著提升JWST/WFSS高红移成团性分析中对宿主晕质量和活动周期等物理量约束的可靠性。

Abstract: We present a framework for inferring the dark matter halo masses of quasars and [O III]-emitting galaxies from JWST/NIRCam Wide Field Slitless Spectroscopy (WFSS) clustering measurements at z approximately 6. Using the FLAMINGO-10k N-body simulation, we construct mock realizations of quasar and galaxy catalogs that incorporate realistic selection functions, spatial coverage, and sensitivity limits matched to the ASPIRE survey. These mocks enable accurate measurements of the quasar-galaxy cross-correlation and galaxy auto-correlation functions, with covariance matrices derived from 1000 realizations that capture both cosmic variance and bin-to-bin correlations. We employ Bayesian inference to fit the correlation functions and infer the minimum halo masses for quasars and galaxies. Our results demonstrate that Poisson pair-count uncertainties, commonly adopted in high-redshift clustering studies, significantly underestimate the true measurement errors. The dominant missing component is cosmic variance: even the diagonal of the full covariance matrix exceeds the Poisson expectation, with off-diagonal bin-to-bin correlations contributing a smaller additional correction. In particular, 1) the commonly used Poisson error on the correlation functions underestimates the true uncertainty by a factor of approximately 3; 2) the uncertainties on the inferred minimum halo masses are underestimated by a factor of approximately 1.5-3 when adopting Poisson errors instead of the full covariance matrix; 3) the inferred QSO halo mass is robust to whether central and satellite [O III]-emitters share a common mass threshold. Our framework provides a more complete error budget for JWST/WFSS clustering analyses, enabling robust constraints on the host halo masses and duty cycles of high-redshift quasars and emission-line galaxies.

</details>


### [41] [New Isocurvature Constraints from JWST UV Luminosity Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11079)
*Raymond T. Co,Sai Chaitanya Tadepalli*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用大尺度宇宙学探针（CMB、BAO、SNe Ia）与小尺度紫外光度函数（UVLF）数据联合限制多种未关联的原初等曲率扰动，首次实现对冷暗物质、重子、中微子密度/速度及暗辐射等成分的模型无关等曲率功率谱的k空间约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在中间尺度（k~0.5–10 Mpc⁻¹, z~4–13）上，对等曲率扰动的尺度依赖性缺乏有效约束，而UVLF可直接探测该范围内的结构形成，填补观测空白。

Method: 采用分段幂律和跑动幂律两种独立参数化形式建模等曲率功率谱，不预先固定谱指数；联合CMB、BAO、SNe Ia与HST/JWST测得的UVLF数据进行贝叶斯分析。

Result: 首次基于UVLF给出多种成分（CDM、baryon、neutrino density/velocity、dark radiation）的模型无关等曲率功率谱k空间约束；68%和95%可信包络在宽k范围内一致，表明结果对幂律形式假设不敏感。

Conclusion: UVLF是限制原初等曲率扰动的有效新探针，尤其适用于中间尺度；所获约束与幂律参数化形式弱相关，增强了结果的稳健性。

Abstract: We constrain uncorrelated primordial isocurvature perturbations using a combination of large- and small-scale cosmological probes, with the small-scale data provided by the ultraviolet luminosity function (UVLF) -- a measure of number density of galaxies as a function of UV brightness. We consider several isocurvature modes, including cold dark matter, baryon, neutrino density, neutrino velocity, and dark radiation perturbations. The isocurvature power spectrum is modeled using two independent parameterizations: a broken power law and a running power law, without fixing the spectral index a priori. Our analysis combines large-scale data from the Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB), baryon acoustic oscillations, and Type Ia supernovae with small-scale constraints from UVLF measurements obtained by \textit{HST} and \textit{JWST}. The UVLF probes matter fluctuations over a continuous range of intermediate scales, $k \sim 0.5$--$10~\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$ over a wide range of redshift $4\lesssim z \lesssim 13$, providing a direct handle on structure formation in a regime where constraints on the scale dependence of isocurvature perturbations remain comparatively limited. Our result represents the first UVLF-based constraint on model-agnostic isocurvature perturbations carried by various components. We construct $68\%$ and $95\%$ credible envelopes in $k$-space for the allowed isocurvature power and find good agreement between the envelopes for the $95\%$ envelope across a wide range of scales, indicating that our constraints are mostly insensitive to the assumed power-law form.

### [42] [FLAMINGO: The thermal history of the Universe from tSZ effect cross-correlations and its dependencies on cosmology and baryon physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11083)
*Jaime Salcido,Tianyi Yang,Ian G. McCarthy,Emily E. Costello,Jonah T. Conley,Willem Elbers,Carlos S. Frenk,Matthieu Schaller,Joop Schaye,Amol Upadhye,Marcel P. van Daalen,Bert Vandenbroucke*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用FLAMINGO宇宙流体动力学模拟，研究了大尺度结构示踪物（如星系、类星体）与热Sunyaev-Zel'dovich（tSZ）信号交叉相关所给出的偏置加权平均电子压力⟨b_h P_e⟩，发现其对S₈参数具有强依赖性，并结合观测数据拟合得到S₈ = 0.72±0.03及特定质量处的归一化重子分数，表明tSZ交叉相关可同时约束宇宙学参数和星系形成反馈模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用tSZ与大尺度结构示踪物的交叉相关来联合约束宇宙学参数（尤其是S₈）和星系形成中的重子反馈物理，弥补小尺度探针（如X射线）的局限性。

Method: 基于FLAMINGO系列大体积、多宇宙学参数与多种重子反馈实现的流体动力学模拟，计算不同红移下⟨b_h P_e⟩及其对S₈的依赖关系，并与SDSS、BOSS、eBOSS、DES、DESI等巡天与Planck tSZ数据的交叉相关观测进行联合拟合。

Result: ⟨b_h P_e⟩ ∝ S₈^ε(z)，其中ε(z)≈3（z=0.1–1）；联合观测拟合得S₈ = 0.72^{+0.03}_{-0.03}，且f_b(10¹³M⊙, z=0.1)/(Ω_b/Ω_m) = 0.10^{+0.09}_{-0.05}；反馈作用反而增强⟨b_h P_e⟩，与小尺度反馈探针趋势相反。

Conclusion: tSZ交叉相关提供了一种新途径，可在大尺度上同时约束S₈类宇宙学参数并检验星系形成反馈模型，热历史d y/dz是关键桥梁。

Abstract: The cross-correlation between tracers of large-scale structure, such as galaxies or quasars, and the thermal Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (tSZ) signal yields a measure of the bias-weighted mean electron pressure, $\langle b_\mathrm{h} P_\mathrm{e} \rangle$, where $b_\mathrm{h}$ is the halo bias and $P_\mathrm{e}$ is the electron pressure. With a model for the bias, one can derive the thermal history, $\mathrm{d}y/\mathrm{d}z$, where $y$ is the Compton parameter and $z$ is redshift. We explore how these quantities depend on redshift, cosmology, and the physics of galaxy formation using the \flamingo\ suite of cosmological hydrodynamical simulations, which spans a range of cosmological parameters and baryonic feedback implementations in volumes of up to $(2.8\,\text{Gpc})^3$. We find that $\langle b_\mathrm{h} P_\mathrm{e} \rangle$ depends steeply on $S_8 \equiv σ_8\sqrt{Ω_\mathrm{m}/0.3}$, with an effective scaling $\langle b_\mathrm{h} P_\mathrm{e} \rangle \propto S_8^{ε(z)}$, where the exponent $ε(z) \approx 3$ over the redshift range $0.1 \leq z \leq 1$. Compared with existing cross-correlation measurements using tracer samples from SDSS, BOSS, eBOSS, DES, and DESI cross-correlated with tSZ measurements from Planck, we find that models with a low-$S_8$ cosmology and strong feedback are preferred, with a joint fit yielding $S_8 = 0.72^{+0.03}_{-0.03}$ and a normalised group-mass halo baryon fraction $f_b(10^{13}\,M_\odot, z=0.1)/(Ω_b/Ω_m) = 0.10^{+0.09}_{-0.05}$ . Contrary to most probes of feedback which sample smaller scales (e.g., X-ray measurements), we show that feedback boosts $\langle b_\mathrm{h} P_\mathrm{e} \rangle$, thus providing a novel test of feedback models. Overall, our results show the thermal history provides a route to jointly constrain cosmological parameters and test models of galaxy formation.

### [43] [A Quantum Gravitational Mechanism for Isotropization of de Sitter Cosmologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11085)
*Stephon Alexander,Bruno Alexandre,Daine L. Danielson,David N. Spergel*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出Lorentzian Chern-Simons-Kodama (CSK) 泛函可被理解为一种具有观测有利性质的引力sphaleron，通过围绕de Sitter鞍点扰动并施加适当量子引力边界条件，发现闭宇宙在动力学上趋向空间各向同性，各向异性模被高斯抑制，从而提供了一种内禀的量子引力各向同化机制；该机制在慢滚暴胀子存在下仍稳健，且仅适用于闭宇宙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释可观测宇宙为何高度各向同性，并探讨其可能源于近乎各向同性的初始状态；利用CSK泛函的性质理解该初始状态。

Method: 将CSK波泛函诠释为引力sphaleron，围绕其主导的de Sitter鞍点进行扰动分析，并施加适当的量子引力边界条件，研究闭宇宙中各向同性演化行为。

Result: 闭宇宙中系统被动力学驱动至空间各向同性，所有各向异性模获得正二次曲率并被高斯压制；sphaleron衰变沿各向同性通道进行；该效应在含慢滚暴胀子时依然稳健；平直或双曲几何中无对应各向同性sphaleron。

Conclusion: Lorentzian CSK泛函可被重新理解为一种手征sphaleron，能自然地为暴胀准备近似各向同性的de Sitter背景；此外，它还可作为一类反常自由对象（包括复化Hartle-Hawking态）的边界泛函。

Abstract: Today, the observable cosmos exhibits a remarkable degree of isotropy and plausibly began in a nearly isotropic initial state. The properties of the Lorentzian Chern-Simons-Kodama (CSK) functional can provide an understanding of this initial state. In gravity with a positive cosmological constant, the Chern-Simons-Kodama (CSK) wavefunctional is an exact, chiral solution of the quantum gravitational constraints. We suggest that the normalizability and other issues with this functional, if interpreted as a proper state of quantum gravity, instead suggest an embedding into a larger quantum gravitational completion, and recast the CSK functional as a gravitational sphaleron with observationally desirable properties. By perturbing around the dominant de Sitter saddle of the wavefunctional with appropriate quantum gravitational boundary conditions, we find that for a closed universe the system is dynamically driven to spatial isotropy, while all anisotropic modes acquire positive quadratic curvature and are Gaussian-suppressed. The decay of this sphaleron therefore proceeds along an isotropic channel, providing an intrinsic quantum-gravitational mechanism for dynamical isotropization. This isotropization effect is robust under the inclusion of a slow-roll inflaton, and no analogous isotropic sphaleron exists for spatially flat or hyperbolic geometries. Taken together, these results recast the Lorentzian CSK functional as a chiral sphaleron that naturally prepares an approximately isotropic de Sitter background for inflation. Beyond this phenomenological study, we further suggest that the CSK functional can be understood as a boundary functional for a class of anomaly-free objects, including a complexified generalization of the Hartle-Hawking state.

### [44] [The Quadruply Lensed Supernova SN 2025wny: Implications for LSST](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11090)

  <summary>Details</summary>
