### [116] [Continuum-Limit HQET LCDAs from Lattice QCD for Tightening B Decay Uncertainties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10946)
*Xue-Ying Han,Hao-Fei Gao,Jun Hua,Xiangdong Ji,Xiangyu Jiang,Cai-Dian Lü,Andreas Schäfer,Jin-Xin Tan,Ji-Hao Wang,Wei Wang,Ji Xu,Yi-Bo Yang,Fu-Wei Zhang,Jian-Hui Zhang,Jia-Lu Zhang,Mu-Hua Zhang,Qi-An Zhang,Shuai Zhao*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过多组模拟和系统误差量化，精确计算了重介子HQET光锥分布振幅（LCDAs），显著降低了理论不确定性，为B介子弱衰变的高精度预言提供了关键支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重介子HQET光锥分布振幅（LCDAs）是B介子弱衰变精密预言的关键，但目前是解释B异常和CP破坏测量的主要理论不确定性来源。

Method: 基于已建立的HQLaMET框架，结合格点QCD对OPE矩的计算，采用多组模拟进行连续极限和物理π质量外推，并通过OPE矩交叉验证结果。

Result: 得到关键反矩结果：λ_B = 0.340(20) GeV 和 σ_B^(1) = 1.685(63)（μ=1 GeV），总不确定度比先前分析减小三倍。

Conclusion: 该工作解决了重介子LCDAs第一性原理预言中的长期瓶颈，推动味物理精度迈入新前沿。

Abstract: Heavy meson HQET light-cone distribution amplitudes (LCDAs) are critical for precision predictions of $B$ meson weak decays, but currently are one of dominant theoretical uncertainties that obscure interpretations of $B$ anomalies and CP-violating measurements. Building on the established HQLaMET framework, supplemented by lattice QCD calculations of the OPE moments, we present a precise lattice QCD calculation of HQET LCDAs by employing multi-ensemble simulations for continuum and physical pion mass extrapolation, quantifying comprehensive systematic errors, and validating results through OPE moment cross-validation. Details of the lattice calculations are provided in a companion paper \cite{HeavymesonDA_long_paper}. Our final results for key inverse moments (at $μ=1$ GeV) are $λ_B=0.340(20)$ GeV and $σ_B^{(1)}=1.685(63)$, with the total uncertainty reduced by a factor of three relative to the previous analysis. These results can greatly reduce the uncertainty in the $B \to K^*$ form factors in the large-recoil region. This work resolves the long-standing bottleneck in first-principles predictions of heavy meson LCDAs, advancing precision flavor physics to new frontiers.

</details>


### [117] [Operator Spectroscopy of Trained Lattice Samplers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11199)
*Moxian Qian*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过将训练后的场空间函数（如流匹配速度、扩散分数或归一化流作用残差）投影到预定义的算子基上，分析了不同格点采样器的内在结构特性，并发现不同采样方法在算子分解中表现出可区分的残差模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上用生成系综评估训练格点采样器，本文转而直接分析采样器所学习的场空间函数本身，以揭示其物理与对称性结构。

Method: 将训练得到的场空间函数（流匹配速度、扩散分数、归一化流残差）投影到由对称性、高斯路径极限、有限体积模和规范协变性预先选定的算子基上，并通过消去特定分量（如零模、低动量模）检验残差变化。

Result: 在2D φ⁴模型中，直流传导教师模型不能仅由局域力基描述；残差可分解为Binder零模分量和最低壳层有限k关联分量；消去P₅(M;t)和φ^⊥_{|n|²=1}分别显著降低对应分量；该投影方法还能区分扩散、逆KL归一化流及规范协变采样器的特征残差结构。

Conclusion: 算子基投影是一种通用、模型与对称性依赖但可复现的诊断工具，能揭示采样器学习到的物理机制，超越系综统计层面，为理解、比较和改进格点生成模型提供新途径。

Abstract: Trained lattice samplers are usually judged by the ensembles they generate. Here we instead analyze the trained field-space function itself: a flow-matching velocity, a diffusion score, or a normalizing-flow action residual. We project these functions onto operator bases fixed before the fit, chosen from symmetry, exact Gaussian path limits, finite-volume modes, and gauge covariance.
  For two-dimensional lattice \(φ^4\), a trained straight-flow teacher is not described by a local force basis alone. After the local transport basis, the residual separates into a zero-mode Binder component and a lowest-shell finite-\(k\) correlator component. The deflated zero-mode polynomial \(P_5(M;t)\) reduces the dominant Binder-tail component, while \(φ^\perp_{|n|^2=1}\) reduces the finite-\(k\) correlator component; wrong-parity, off-zero-mode, and random controls do not produce the same reductions.
  The same projection distinguishes other sampler classes. Diffusion follows the force-resolvent ordering predicted by the free theory, reverse-KL normalizing-flow collapse appears as a forbidden odd zero-mode residual, and gauge-equivariant teachers are resolved by Wilson-loop-force tangent directions. The operator basis is model- and symmetry-dependent, but the test is common: project the trained field-space function and retain sectors that lower held-out residuals and pass the available controls.

</details>
